import json

def route_response(response: str) -> str:
    trimmed = response.strip()

    try:
        json.loads(trimmed)
        return "JSON"
    except Exception:
        pass

    if any(keyword in trimmed.lower() for keyword in ["error", "exception", "traceback"]):
        return "ERROR"

    if any(trimmed.startswith(kw) for kw in ["def ", "print(", "import ", "for ", "while ", "if "]):
        return "CODE"

    if trimmed.lower().startswith("echo") or len(trimmed.splitlines()) == 1:
        return "ECHO"

    return "UNKNOWN"

from core.system_controller import process_command

def process_batch(batch_data: list) -> list:
    results = []

    for item in batch_data:
        parancs = item.get("parancs")
        if not parancs:
            results.append({"error": "Hi√°nyz√≥ 'parancs' kulcs", "input": item})
            continue

        result = process_command(parancs)
        results.append({"parancs": parancs, "eredmeny": result})

    return results

import io
import sys
import traceback

def execute_python(code: str) -> str:
    old_stdout = sys.stdout
    redirected_output = sys.stdout = io.StringIO()

    try:
        compiled = compile(code, "<string>", "exec")
        exec(compiled, {})
        result = redirected_output.getvalue()
        return result if result else "‚úÖ Futott, de nincs kimenet."
    except Exception:
        return f"‚ùå Hiba:\n{traceback.format_exc()}"
    finally:
        sys.stdout = old_stdout

async def handle_input(command: str):

        return run_command(command[4:].strip())

    elif command.startswith("FILE:"):

    elif command.startswith("CODE:"):
        return execute_python(command[5:].strip())

    else:
        return "‚ö†Ô∏è Ismeretlen parancst√≠pus."

# modules/code_runner.py
import io
import sys
import traceback

def execute_python(code: str) -> str:
    old_stdout = sys.stdout
    redirected_output = sys.stdout = io.StringIO()

    try:
        compiled = compile(code, "<string>", "exec")
        exec(compiled, {})
        result = redirected_output.getvalue()
        return result if result else "‚úÖ Futott, de nincs kimenet."
    except Exception:
        return f"‚ùå Hiba:\n{traceback.format_exc()}"
    finally:
        sys.stdout = old_stdout

# agent_core.py
import logging
from modules.code_runner import execute_python

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)

async def handle_input(command: str):
    logging.info(f"üì• Kapott parancs: {command}")

    if command.startswith("CMD:"):
        return run_command(command[4:].strip())  # TODO

    elif command.startswith("FILE:"):
        return handle_file_command(command[5:].strip())  # TODO

    elif command.startswith("CODE:"):
        return execute_python(command[5:].strip())

    else:
        return "‚ö†Ô∏è Ismeretlen parancst√≠pus."

import asyncio
from chatgpt_automation.chatgpt_automation import ChatGPT
import json

with open("config.json") as f:
    config = json.load(f)

chat = ChatGPT(api_key=config["api_key"])

async def main():
    print("ü§ñ Project S ‚Äì ChatGPT local agent online")
    while True:
        try:
            command = input(">> ")
            if command.startswith("CODE:"):
                response = chat.ask(command[5:].strip())
                print("üß† Kimenet:\n", response)
            else:
                print("‚ö†Ô∏è Csak CODE: parancs t√°mogatott jelenleg.")
        except KeyboardInterrupt:
            print("üëã Kil√©p√©s...")
            break

if __name__ == "__main__":
    asyncio.run(main())

import io
import sys
import traceback

def execute_python(code: str) -> str:
    old_stdout = sys.stdout
    redirected_output = sys.stdout = io.StringIO()
    
    try:
        exec(code, {})
        return redirected_output.getvalue() or "‚úÖ Lefutott, de nem volt kimenet."
    except Exception:
        return f"‚ùå Hiba:\n{traceback.format_exc()}"
    finally:
        sys.stdout = old_stdout

import os
import subprocess
import asyncio
import websockets
from chatgpt_automation.chatgpt_automation import ChatGPTAutomation

chat = None

async def command_handler(websocket):
    global chat
    print("[S] ü§ñ System Controller akt√≠v.")
    try:
        chat = ChatGPTAutomation()
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[S] ‚ö†Ô∏è Nem siker√ºlt inicializ√°lni a ChatGPTAutomation-t: {e}")
        chat = None

    try:
        async for message in websocket:
            print(f"[S] üì© Parancs √©rkezett: {message}")
            if message.startswith("CMD:"):
                cmd = message[4:].strip()
                print(f"[S] ‚öôÔ∏è  V√©grehajt√°s: {cmd}")

                try:
                    output = subprocess.getoutput(cmd)
                    print(f"[S] üì§ Kimenet:\n{output}")
                except Exception as e:
                    output = f"Hiba: {e}"

                if chat:
                    try:
                        chat.send_message(f"üì§ CMD Output:\n{output}")
                        print("[S] üìù Kimenet visszak√ºldve a GPT-nek.")
                    except Exception as e:
                        print(f"[S] ‚ùå Nem siker√ºlt visszak√ºldeni a kimenetet: {e}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"[S] ‚ùå Hiba a websocket kapcsolatban: {e}")

async def main():
    async with websockets.serve(command_handler, "localhost", 8765):
        print("[S] üß† WebSocket parancsfogad√≥ fut (8765)")
        await asyncio.Future()  # v√©gtelen fut√°s

if __name__ == "__main__":
    asyncio.run(main())

[2025-04-21 19:07:14] ASSISTANT: Ez azt jelenti, hogy a rendszer m√©g mindig nem ismeri fel a JSON strukt√∫r√°t, tov√°bbra is csak visszaism√©tli.

Copy
import json

def route_response(response: str) -> str:
    trimmed = response.strip()

    try:
        json.loads(trimmed)
        return "JSON"
    except Exception:
        pass

    if any(keyword in trimmed.lower() for keyword in ["error", "exception", "traceback"]):
        return "ERROR"

    if any(trimmed.startswith(kw) for kw in ["def ", "print(", "import ", "for ", "while ", "if "]):
        return "CODE"

    if trimmed.lower().startswith("echo") or len(trimmed.splitlines()) == 1:
        return "ECHO"

    return "UNKNOWN"

def handle_response(response: str):
    response_type = route_response(response)
    print("DEBUG ‚Äì Routed as:", response_type)

    if response_type == "ECHO":
        return  # Ne k√ºldj vissza semmit

    if response_type == "ERROR":
        print("‚ö† Hiba t√∂rt√©nt:", response)

    if response_type in ["JSON", "CODE"]:
        # Itt t√∂rt√©nhet a tov√°bbl√©p√©s a parancsv√©grehajt√°sra

def process_batch(batch_data: list) -> list:
    results = []

        parancs = item.get("parancs")
        if not parancs:
            results.append({"error": "Hi√°nyz√≥ 'parancs' kulcs", "input": item})
            continue

        result = process_command(parancs)

    return results

# ai_command_handler.py

class AICommandHandler:

    def __init__(self):
        self.iteration_active = False

    def _parse_command_params(self, command: str):
        parts = command.split()
        return parts[0], parts[1:]

    def execute_command(self, command: str):
        base_cmd, params = self._parse_command_params(command)

        if base_cmd.lower() == "continue":
            if self.iteration_active:
                return "Iteration already in progress."
            self.iteration_active = True
            return self._start_iteration()
        
        elif base_cmd.lower() == "stop":
            self.iteration_active = False
            return "Iteration stopped."

        return f"Unknown command: {base_cmd}"

    def _start_iteration(self):
        # itt mehet egy loop, replay manager, stb.
        results = []
        for i in range(3):
            results.append(f"Cycle {i} OK")
        return "\n".join(results)

import json
import os

MEMORY_FILE = 'memory.json'

def load_memory():
    if not os.path.exists(MEMORY_FILE):
        return {}
    with open(MEMORY_FILE, 'r') as f:
        return json.load(f)

def save_memory(data):
    with open(MEMORY_FILE, 'w') as f:
        json.dump(data, f, indent=2)

def remember(key, value):
    data = load_memory()
    data[key] = value
    save_memory(data)

def recall(key):
    data = load_memory()
    return data.get(key, None)

import subprocess

def process_command(command):
    command = command.strip()

    if command.startswith("CMD:"):
        raw_command = command[len("CMD:"):].strip()

        if raw_command.startswith("FORCE:"):
            raw_command = raw_command[len("FORCE:"):].strip()

        try:
            output = subprocess.check_output(raw_command, shell=True, text=True)
            print(output.strip() + "\n>>END<<")
        except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
            print(f"[ERROR] {e}\n>>END<<")
        return

    # ide

import subprocess

def process_command(command):
    command = command.strip()

    if command.startswith("CMD:"):
        raw_command = command[len("CMD:"):].strip()

        if raw_command.startswith("FORCE:"):
            raw_command = raw_command[len("FORCE:"):].strip()

        try:
            output = subprocess.check_output(raw_command, shell=True, text=True)
            print(output.strip() + "\n>>END<<")
        except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
            print(f"[ERROR] {e}\n>>END<<")
        return

    print("[ERROR] Unrecognized command type.\n>>END<<")

def sanitize_cmd_input(command: str) -> str:
    if command.startswith("CMD:"):
        command = command[len("CMD:"):].strip()

    if command.startswith("FORCE:"):
        command = command[len("FORCE:"):].strip()

    return command

[2025-04-23 18:34:40] ASSISTANT: ‚úîÔ∏è Az ism√©telt WebSocket 1011 hiba azt er≈ës√≠ti meg, hogy a szerver oldalon fut√°si hiba t√∂rt√©nik a k√©zfog√°s ut√°n ‚Äì a kapcsolat l√©trej√∂n, de valami azonnal elrontja.
üìå R√©szletes magyar√°zat:

N√©zd meg a legut√≥bbi parancsokat is ‚Äì lehet, hogy egy hib√°s CODE: blokk vagy CMD parancs feldolgoz√°s√°n√°l sz√°ll el a szerver.

[2025-04-23 18:34:40] ASSISTANT: Ez a GitHub Copilot logikus elemz√©s√©b≈ël sz√°rmazik, √©s azt jelzi, hogy az ai_command_handler.py f√°jlban m√©g nincs k√©sz a parancsparam√©ter-kezel√©s √©s az iter√°ci√≥s logika, de az AI elkezdte fel√©p√≠teni a t√°mogat√°st hozz√°.
üîç Mit l√°tunk a napl√≥ban?
A Copilot pr√≥b√°lja meg√©rteni, mi az a "Continue to iterate?" t√≠pus√∫ parancs.
T√∂bb szinten keres:
Param√©terparsing (_parse_command_params)
execute_command() met√≥dus b≈ëv√≠t√©se t√∂bb param√©terrel
Iter√°ci√≥kezel√©shez kapcsol√≥d√≥ logika hi√°nyzik
A k√≥dalapban van m√°r infrastrukt√∫ra a parancsok feldolgoz√°s√°ra, de konkr√©t iter√°ci√≥s parancs (pl. "Continue" vagy "Repeat") kezel√©se nincs implement√°lva.
‚úÖ Mit tegy√ºnk most?
Ha szeretn√©d, √©n gyorsan be√©p√≠tem az iter√°ci√≥kezel√©st. P√©ld√°ul √≠gy:
python
Copy
# ai_command_handler.py

class AICommandHandler:

    def __init__(self):
        self.iteration_active = False

    def _parse_command_params(self, command: str):
        parts = command.split()
        return parts[0], parts[1:]

    def execute_command(self, command: str):
        base_cmd, params = self._parse_command_params(command)

        if base_cmd.lower() == "continue":
            if self.iteration_active:
                return "Iteration already in progress."
            self.iteration_active = True
            return self._start_iteration()
        
        elif base_cmd.lower() == "stop":
            self.iteration_active = False
            return "Iteration stopped."

        return f"Unknown command: {base_cmd}"

    def _start_iteration(self):
        # itt mehet egy loop, replay manager, stb.
        results = []
        for i in range(3):
            results.append(f"Cycle {i} OK")
        return "\n".join(results)
‚ûï Ez mit ad hozz√°?
Continue parancs elind√≠t egy m≈±veletsorozatot (3 ciklus)
Stop megszak√≠tja
K√©s≈ëbb b≈ëv√≠thet≈ë √∫j parancsokkal, felt√©telekkel
Sz√≥lj, ha be√©p√≠ts√ºk ezt k√∂z√∂sen a ai_command_handler.py-be, vagy ha m√°shogy akarod kezelni az iter√°ci√≥s parancsokat!
[2025-04-23 18:34:40] ASSISTANT: ‚úîÔ∏è Visszaigazolva:
A rendszer helyesen reag√°lt a nem l√©tez≈ë mappa list√°z√°s√°ra.
√úzenet:
css

import os

class AICommandHandler:

    def __init__(self):
        pass

    # Egy parancs futtat√°sa
    def run_cmd(self, command: str):
        print(f"Futtat√°s: {command}")
        os.system(command)

    # T√∂bb parancs futtat√°sa
    def run_multiple_commands(self, commands: list):
        results = []
        for cmd in commands:
            print(f"Futtat√°s: {cmd}")
            result = os.system(cmd)
            results.append({"command": cmd, "result": result})
        return results

class AICommandHandler:

    def __init__(self):
        pass

    # Egy parancs futtat√°sa
    def run_cmd(self, command: str):
        print(f"Futtat√°s: {command}")
        os.system(command)

    # T√∂bb parancs futtat√°sa
    def run_multiple_commands(self, commands: list):
        results = []

            result = os.system(cmd)
            results.append({"command": cmd, "result": result})
        return results

import os

class AICommandHandler:

    def __init__(self):
        pass

    # Egy parancs futtat√°sa
    def run_cmd(self, command: str):
        # Ellen≈ërizz√ºk, hogy a parancs CMD: el≈ëtaggal kezd≈ëdik
        if command.startswith("CMD:"):
            command = command[4:].strip()  # Lev√°gjuk az el≈ëtagot
            print(f"Futtat√°s: {command}")
            os.system(command)
        else:
            print("√ârv√©nytelen parancs! A parancsnak 'CMD:' el≈ëtaggal kell kezd≈ëdnie.")

    # T√∂bb parancs futtat√°sa
    def run_multiple_commands(self, commands: list):
        results = []
        for cmd in commands:
            # Ha a parancs kezd≈ëdik 'CMD:'-vel, akkor feldolgozzuk
            if cmd.startswith("CMD:"):
                command = cmd[4:].strip()
                print(f"Futtat√°s: {command}")
                result = os.system(command)
                results.append({"command": command, "result": result})
            else:
                print("√ârv√©nytelen parancs! A parancsnak 'CMD:' el≈ëtaggal kell kezd≈ëdnie.")
        return results

# Tesztel√©s
handler = AICommandHandler()

# Egyedi parancs
handler.run_cmd("CMD: echo Hello World")

# T√∂bb parancs
parancsok = [
    "CMD: echo Els≈ë parancs",
    "CMD: echo M√°sodik parancs",
    "CMD: date /t"
]
results = handler.run_multiple_commands(parancsok)

# Eredm√©nyek nyomon k√∂vet√©se
for result in results:
    print(f"Parancs: {result['command']} | Eredm√©ny: {result['result']}")

Let me modify the AICommandHandler to provide better feedback for file redirection commands, since they typically don't produce direct output but do perform an action:

ai_command_handler.py+30-1
I've modified the _run_system_command method to provide better feedback for file redirection commands. Now, when a command contains redirection operators ('>', '>>', '<') and executes successfully but has no direct output, it will:

Try to extract the target filename from the redirection
Check if the file exists after the operation
Provide a meaningful message about the file operation's success
